2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 To enable it, first install UCX (conda install -c conda-forge ucx).
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 Afterwards, set the environment variables
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 OMPI_MCA_pml=ucx OMPI_MCA_osc=ucx
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 before launching your MPI processes.
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameters in the command line:
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 mpiexec --mca pml ucx --mca osc ucx ...
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 On Linux, Open MPI is built with UCC support but it is disabled by default.
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 To enable it, first install UCC (conda install -c conda-forge ucc).
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 Afterwards, set the environment variables
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 OMPI_MCA_coll_ucc_enable=1
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 before launching your MPI processes.

2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 before launching your MPI processes.

2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 mpiexec --mca opal_cuda_support 1 ...

2024-11-11T17:37:32Z #11 285.4 UCX. Please consult UCX documentation for further details.
